25:T722,<entryFree id="n18790" key="سَبَقٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">سَبَقٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A stake,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wager, that is laid between the persons concerned in a race,</hi> (T, S, O, Mgh, * Msb, * K,) and <hi rend="ital">in a shooting-match; in the former case taken by</hi> [<hi rend="ital">the owner of</hi>] <hi rend="ital">the one that outstrips;</hi> (T, TA:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n18790-1" target="سُبْقَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n18791"/></foreign> signifies the same: (K:) pl. of the former <foreign lang="ar">أَسْبَاقٌ</foreign>. (O, K.) It is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">لَا سَبَقَ إِلَّا فِى خُفٍّ أَوْ حَافِرٍ أَوْ نَصْلٍ</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">There shall be no stake,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wager, except in the case of</hi> the racing of <hi rend="ital">camels, or of horses</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mules</hi> or <hi rend="ital">asses, or in the case of</hi> [<hi rend="ital">the arrowhead</hi> or <hi rend="ital">lance-head,</hi> i. e.] shooting or casting [the lance]: for all these affairs are preparations for engaging in fight with the enemy; and mules and asses are included because they carry the baggage of the army. (O, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  The <hi rend="ital">lesson</hi> of a boy, <hi rend="ital">that is learned each day in the school;</hi> also called <foreign lang="ar">إِمَامٌ</foreign>. (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">ام</foreign>.)    </entryFree>26:T1ccf,<entryFree id="n18784" key="سَبَقَهُ" type="main">
